25/08/25 14:50:21 §aalue. Heres a detailed breakdown
25/08/25 14:50:23 <MrTracker> §a> of the process:1.  Padding: The input message is
25/08/25 14:50:23 §a padded to ensure its length i
25/08/25 14:50:25 <MrTracker> §a> s a multiple of 512 bits. Padding involves adding
25/08/25 14:50:25 §a a 1 bit to the end of the me
25/08/25 14:50:28 <MrTracker> §a> ssage followed by 0 bits until the message lengt
25/08/25 14:50:28 §ah is 64 bits less than a mult
25/08/25 14:50:30 <MrTracker> §a> iple of 512. The final 64 bits represent the orig
25/08/25 14:50:30 §ainal message length in binary.
25/08/25 14:50:31 <MrTracker> §a> 2.  Parsing: The padded message is divided into 
25/08/25 14:50:31 §a512-bit blocks.3.  Initializa
25/08/25 14:50:33 <MrTracker> §a> tion: SHA-256 uses eight 32-bit hash values as i
25/08/25 14:50:33 §anitial state (H0 to H7). These a
25/08/25 14:50:37 <MrTracker> §a> re predefined constants.4.  Processing Blocks: 
25/08/25 14:50:37 §aEach 512-bit block is processed
25/08/25 14:50:40 <MrTracker> §a>  through 64 rounds. Each round involves the f
25/08/25 14:50:40 §aollowing:    *   Message Schedule
25/08/25 14:50:40 <MrTracker> §a> : The 512-bit block is expanded into 64 32-bit w
25/08/25 14:50:40 §aords (W0 to W63). The first 16 w
25/08/25 14:50:41 <MrTracker> §a> ords are derived directly from the block. The r
25/08/25 14:50:41 §aemaining words are calculated usi
25/08/25 14:50:43 <MrTracker> §a> ng a specific formula involving previous words 
25/08/25 14:50:43 §aand bitwise operations (rotations
25/08/25 14:50:45 <MrTracker> §a>  shifts XOR).    *   Compression Function: This is
25/08/25 14:50:45 §a the core of SHA-256. It u
25/08/25 14:50:47 <MrTracker> §a> ses the message schedule words the current h
25/08/25 14:50:47 §aash values (H0 to H7) and a set of
25/08/25 14:50:49 <MrTracker> §a>  64 constant values (K0 to K63). The compressi
25/08/25 14:50:49 §aon function involves a series of b
25/08/25 14:50:52 <MrTracker> §a> itwise operations (AND OR XOR NOT shifts rotatio
25/08/25 14:50:52 §ans) and additions updating
25/08/25 14:50:53 <MrTracker> §a>  the hash values in each round.5.  Updating Has
25/08/25 14:50:53 §ah Values: After processing each
25/08/25 14:50:55 <MrTracker> §a>  512-bit block the resulting hash values from t
25/08/25 14:50:55 §ahe compression function are adde
25/08/25 14:50:57 <MrTracker> §a> d to the initial hash values (or the hash values
25/08/25 14:50:57 §a from the previous block).6.
25/08/25 14:50:59 <MrTracker> §a> Finalization: After processing all blocks the fina
25/08/25 14:50:59 §al hash values (H0 to H7) are

25/08/25 14:51:01 §ahash.The bitwise operations and co
25/08/25 14:51:03 <MrTracker> §a> nstants are designed to provide diffusion and 
25/08/25 14:51:03 §aconfusion making it computational
25/08/25 14:51:05 <MrTracker> §a> ly infeasible to reverse the process and find t
25/08/25 14:51:05 §ahe original message from the hash
